## Types Documentation

### enum EMVAppFlowCapabilityBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CT_FORCE_RISK_MANAGEMENT | =0|  Perform risk management in every case.  |
| EMV_CT_BLACKLIST | =1|  Support of blacklist (exception list), the callback set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_CHECK_LOG_HOTLIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-check-log-hotlist)) will be invoked 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_HOTLST_LOG_CALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-hotlst-log-callback) and [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_TRANSACTION_LOG | =2|  Support transaction log, the callback set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_CHECK_LOG_HOTLIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-check-log-hotlist)) will be invoked 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_HOTLST_LOG_CALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-hotlst-log-callback) and [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_PIN_BYPASS | =3|  PIN bypass supported  |
| EMV_CT_FORCE_ONLINE | =4|  Feature "Force online" supported  |
| EMV_CT_FORCE_ACCEPTANCE | =5|  Feature "Force acceptance" supported  |
| EMV_CT_CASH_SUPPORT | =8|  Support of cash transactions  |
| EMV_CT_CASHBACK_SUPPORT | =9|  Support of cashback transactions  |
| EMV_CT_CHECK_INCONS_TRACK2_PAN | =10|  Check consistency of track2 equivalent data ([EMV_TRACK2_EQUIVALENT_DATA](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-track2-equivalent-data)) provided by ICC. 

 Mandated for MasterCard and Amex. 

 Validate format and that contents matches to [EMV_PAN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-pan) and [EMV_EXPIRATION_DATE](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-expiration-date). 

 See also [EMV_CT_FALLBACK_ON_INCONS_TRACK2](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-fallback-on-incons-track2).  |
| EMV_CT_CONF_AMOUNT_PIN | =11|  Confirm amount and enter PIN in one display. 

 Invoking callback for amount confirmation depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_AMOUNT_CONF](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-amount-conf). 

 May be deactivated by [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks).  |
| EMV_CT_DOMESTIC_CHECK | =12|  the callback set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_LOCAL_CHECKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-local-checks)) will be called. 

 Needs to be activated per transaction by [EMV_CT_TXNOP_LOCAL_CHCK_CALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-local-chck-callback). 

 May be deactivated by [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks).  |
| EMV_CT_TRANSACTION_TYPE_17_FOR_CASH | =13|  Enable mapping of transaction type for cash transaction from 0x01 to 0x17  |
| EMV_CT_CHECK_INCONS_TRACK2_NO_EXP | =14|  Check consistency of track2 equivalent data ([EMV_TRACK2_EQUIVALENT_DATA](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-track2-equivalent-data)) provided by ICC. 

 Mandated for MasterCard and Amex. 

 Validate format and that contents matches to [EMV_PAN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-pan)

 Only effective if [EMV_CT_CHECK_INCONS_TRACK2_PAN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-check-incons-track2-pan) is deactivated. See also [EMV_CT_FALLBACK_ON_INCONS_TRACK2](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-fallback-on-incons-track2).  |
| EMV_CT_TRANSACTION_TYPE_30_FOR_PREAUTH | 15|  Amex Pre-Authorization with transaction type 30 Use [EMV_ADK_TRAN_TYPE_AMEX_PREAUTH](group___t_r_a_n_s___t_y_p_e_s.md#define-emv-adk-tran-type-amex-preauth) for pre-authorization resp. reservation transactions. The modified transaction type is used towards card and put out in tag 9C.  |
| EMV_CT_REFERRAL_AFTER_TXN | =16|  In case voice referral is required: Chip transaction is terminated with AAC. Referral transaction is performed subsequently as "CardNotPresent" (German handling).  |
| EMV_CT_DCC_CHECK | =17|  Enable DCC (Dynamic currency conversion). 

 Invocation depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks), [EMV_CT_TXNOP_DCC_CALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-dcc-callback), and [EMV_CT_TXNOP_DCC_CALLBACK_ALWAYS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-dcc-callback-always).  |
| EMV_CT_REFUND_CONFIRM_AMOUNT | =18|  Confirm amount during refund transaction 

 Invoking callback for amount confirmation depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_AMOUNT_CONF](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-amount-conf) and [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks).  |
| EMV_CT_USE_CFG_APPL_NAME | =19|  Use configured application name instead of EMVCo rule (9F12 prior to 50 prior to configured). Effective for cardholder's application selection.  |
| EMV_CT_FALLBACK_ON_INCONS_TRACK2 | =20|  Valid only in case of activated [EMV_CT_CHECK_INCONS_TRACK2_PAN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-check-incons-track2-pan). 

 If activated: Check will be done before Cardholder Verification. In case of fail EMV ADK will process fallback handling (may result in [EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-fallback)). E.g. required for German dcpos 2.4, may be used for "M/Chip Functional Architecture", AMEX ED-031 in test plan ver. 4.2. 

 If not activated: Check will be done just before processing 1st cryptogram. If fail: GENAC1 will be requested with AAC. E.g. required for MasterCard REQ22, AMEX ED-031 in Swedish AMEX test plan 1.0.  |
| EMV_CT_AMOUNT_CONFIRM_ON_SIGNATURE | =21|  Customer amount confirmation in case of CVM signature 

 Invoking callback for amount confirmation depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_AMOUNT_CONF](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-amount-conf) and [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks).  |
| EMV_CT_SDA_SELECTED_TVR_ON | =22|  Activate the support of the TVR byte SDA selected, introduced in Nov 2013 for kernels not yet supporting this feature, configurable per AID (for kernels supporting this it'll eb always activated, config is don't care)  |
| EMV_CT_CASHBACK_OFFLINE_SUPPORT | =23|  If set cash back transactions are not automatically forced online.  |
| EMV_CT_REFUND_PROCESSING_RESTRICTIONS | =24|  Perform Processing restrictions for Refund transactions (French Refund Requirements).  |
| EMV_CT_REFUND_NO_GENERATE_AC | =25|  Do not perform Generate AC when finishing Refund transactions (French Refund Requirements).  |
| EMV_CT_REFUND_FLOW_INTERAC | =26|  Perform full EMV transaction although transaction type is refund.  |
| EMV_CT_REFUND_NO_ZERO_AMOUNT | =27|  Do NOT set the amount to zero in CDOL1 for Refund transactions with Generate AC.  |
| EMV_CT_DPAS_DATA_STORAGE_SUPPORT | =28|  Support of Data Storage for D-PAS Connect. Useful only for Discover AIDs.  |
| EMV_CT_DPAS_EXTENDED_LOGGING_SUPPORT | =29|  Support of Extended Logging for D-PAS Connect. Useful only for Discover AIDs.  |
| EMV_CT_DPAS_CDCVM_SUPPORT | =30|  Support of Consumer Device CVM for D-PAS Connect. Useful only for Discover AIDs.  |
| EMV_CT_APP_FLOW_VISA_QUASI_CASH | =31|  Convert transaction type from '01' to '11' indicating VISA Quasi Cash. Use in conjunction with [EMV_CT_APPLIDATA_TYPE](group___d_e_f___c_o_n_f___a_p_p_l_i.md#typedef-emv-ct-applidata-type). TxnTypesCash if AUC checks shall be applied, that is both values '01' and '11' should be set.  |
| EMV_CT_APP_FLOW_CASHBACK_TRANS_TYPE_00 | =32|  Convert transaction type from '09' to '00' indicating Cashback. This is a VISA L3 requirement for new L3 test cases. Use in conjunction with [EMV_CT_APPLIDATA_TYPE](group___d_e_f___c_o_n_f___a_p_p_l_i.md#typedef-emv-ct-applidata-type). TxnTypesCashback if AUC checks shall be applied, that is both values '00' and '09' should be set.  |
| EMV_CTLS_DOM_NO_FINAL_SELECT | =0|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Do not perform the final select if the AID belongs to a nonEMV/Domestic kernel  |
| EMV_CTLS_LOA_ENABLE | =1|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Enable list of applications processing for this AID (per default not recommended for CTLS txns because directory file is available)  |
| EMV_CTLS_CASH_SUPPORT | =2|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Support of cash transactions  |
| EMV_CTLS_CASHBACK_SUPPORT | =3|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Support of cashback transactions  |
| EMV_CTLS_OMIT_NOT_ALLOWED_SELECTION | =4|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Omit not allowed candidates already during Entry Point selection process, e.g. above CTLS transaction limit. However: Warning: The EP defines Contactless transaction Limit >=, while MasterCard PP3 defines it as >. So do not set it for MasterCard AIDs  |
| EMV_CTLS_FORCE_ENTRY_POINT | =5|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Force Entry Point processing of the former EMVCo Entry Point specification  |
| EMV_CTLS_FORCE_KERNEL_USAGE | =6|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Force Kernel ID to be used, even if EP tag 9F2A is available  |
| EMV_CTLS_LIST_OF_AIDS_IF_PPSE_MISSING_ONLY | =7|  (Vel: y VFI: y) List of AIDs method only if PPSE directory does not exist in a card with the corresponding AID. Precondition: [EMV_CTLS_LOA_ENABLE](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-loa-enable) is set.  |
| EMV_CTLS_LIST_OF_AIDS_IF_PPSE_FAILED_ONLY | =8|  (Vel: n VFI: y) List of AIDs method only if PPSE directory exists in the card but a response for PPSE request was badly formatted and PPSE stage failed. Precondition: [EMV_CTLS_LOA_ENABLE](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-loa-enable) is set.  |
| EMV_CTLS_CARD_READ_TXN_ZERO_AMOUNT | =9|  (Vel: y VFI: y) If this bit is set then the reader will send an amount of zero to the card for card read transactions, otherwise the reader will send the normal amount  |
| EMV_CTLS_SKIP_CARDSELECTION_APPS | =10|  (Vel: y VFI: n) If this bit is set this AID will be skipped if requiring explicit cardholder selection  |
| EMV_CTLS_SKIP_TXN_LIMIT_CHECK | =11|  (Vel: y VFI: n) If this bit is set for this AID the transaction limit check will be skipped and the AID remains in the candidate list  |
| EMV_CTLS_FORCE_ONLINE | =12|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Feature "Force online" supported  |
| EMV_CTLS_WAIT_CARD_REMOVAL_END | =13|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Wait for card removal at the end of an EMV transaction before returning to application (on TC, AAC and ARQC --> Card Read Complete)  |
| EMV_CTLS_START_REMOVAL_DETECTION | =14|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Start card removal procedure after kernel processing. This enables the service [SDIClient::emvCtlsCardRemoval](group__sdiemvctls.md#function-emvctlscardremoval). 

 Only effective on deactivated [EMV_CTLS_WAIT_CARD_REMOVAL_END](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-wait-card-removal-end) |
| EMV_CTLS_EP_EXTENDED_SELECTION | =15|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Enable the Entry Point extended selection (9F29 is used if present on ICC)  |
| EMV_CTLS_MULTIPLE_AID_KERNEL_ID | =16|  (Vel: y VFI: n) byte 2 of kernel id is used to store multiple configurations of same kernel Id-AID pair. If this flag is set the 3rd byte of the kernel id is set to zero in the Terminal Candidate List which is presented to the EntryPoint while the original value is used towards application interface.  |
| EMV_CTLS_ENABLE_OFFLINE_CASHBACK | =17|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Do not apply business rule: "Cash back is online only". Instead rely on terminal and card risk management. Anyhow the application might force the transaction online by transaction flow option. 
**Caution**: For Visa like schemes (Visa, Visa-AP, Discover and UPI) this flag has a different effect: It suppresses the mandory reduction of the floor limit to zero.  |
| EMV_CTLS_RESET_TXN_TYPE | =18|  (Vel: y VFI: n) A custom transaction type ('9C') might be used during kernel processing in a virtual terminal for card read transactions. Therefore tag '9C' has to be configured using [EMVConf::setAdditionalTags()](structvfisdi_1_1_e_m_v_conf.md#function-setadditionaltags) If this flag is raised the transaction type in the kernel database will be reset after completion (e.g. to '20' for refund) in order to hide this modification from the outside world (vouchers, host messages)  |
| EMV_CTLS_CFG_APPL_NAME | =19|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Always use default application label [EMV_CTLS_APPLIDATA_SCHEME_SPECIFIC_STRUCT::DefaultApplicationName_DFAB22](struct_e_m_v___c_t_l_s___a_p_p_l_i_d_a_t_a___s_c_h_e_m_e___s_p_e_c_i_f_i_c___s_t_r_u_c_t.md#variable-defaultapplicationname-dfab22) in result data [EMV_CTLS_TRANSRES_STRUCT::AppName](struct_e_m_v___c_t_l_s___t_r_a_n_s_r_e_s___s_t_r_u_c_t.md#variable-appname) |
| EMV_CTLS_CARD_READ_SKIP_TXN_LIMIT_CHECK | =20|  B3b5: (Vel: y VFI: n) If this bit is set for this AID the transaction limit check will be skipped for card read transactions and the AID remains in the candidate list  |




EMV flow capability bit numbers 


### enum EMVKernelAppFlowCapabilityBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CTLS_READ_BALANCE_BEFORE_GAC_MK | =0|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Feature Read Balance before GenAC  |
| EMV_CTLS_READ_BALANCE_AFTER_GAC_MK | =1|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Feature Read Balance after GenAC  |
| EMV_CTLS_ENABLE_DATA_EXCHANGE_MK | =2|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Enable DataExchange  |
| EMV_CTLS_TRANSACTION_TYPE_17_FOR_CASH_MK | =3|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Enable mapping of transaction type for cash transaction from 0x01 to 0x17  |
| EMV_CTLS_CARD_READ_ACTION_ANALYSIS_MK | =4|  (Vel: y VFI: n) On card read transa  |
| EMV_CTLS_STATUS_CHECK_ENABLE_VK | =0|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Enable status check for one single unit of currency (1$ txn is going online for status check)  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CHECK_ENABLE_SKIP_VK | =1|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Enable zero check for zero amount transaction, Option 2: skip AID for zero amount txns. Can't be combined with Option 2 in B1b3  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CHECK_ENABLE_ONLINE_VK | =2|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Enable zero check for zero amount transaction, Option 1: going online for zero amount txns. Can't be combined with Option 1 in B1b2. This is the default option. This is the prioritary option if both options are set  |
| EMV_CTLS_CHECK_INCONS_TRACK2_PAN_VK | =3|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Check consistency of track2 equivalent data ([EMV_TRACK2_EQUIVALENT_DATA](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-track2-equivalent-data)) provided by ICC. Validate format and that contents matches to [EMV_PAN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-pan). Visa Europe stuff VppT  |
| EMV_CTLS_CASHBACK_NOT_FORCED_CVM_VK | =4|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Per default cashback transactions require CVM and are forced online by setting floorlimit to 0, you can use standard CVM limit and floorlimit if you set this flag  |
| EMV_CTLS_ALERT_TONE_ON_DECLINE_VK | =6|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Per default the tone indicates if card read successful or not. Outcome of the transaction is not indicated. With this option an additional alert tone is sounded in case transaction is declined.  |
| EMV_CTLS_GET_DATA_9F68_VK | =7|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Card Read Flow initiated with [EMV_TXN_READ_CARD_DATA](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-read-card-data) for retrieval of tag 9F68 (Card Additional Processes)  |
| EMV_CTLS_ENABLE_TAGS_AT_GPO_VK | =8|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Apply workaround that Visa kernel up to version 2.1.5 accepts certain tags at GPO step. These are 9F07 & 5F28 for instance.  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CHECK_DISABLE_VK | =9|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Disable Visa zero check  |
| EMV_CTLS_ODO_SUPPORT_VK | =11|  (Vel: y VFI n) VK2.2.3 only: Enable Offline Data Authentication for online transactions (ODO) according "Visa ODA for qVSDC Online Specification". Note: To enable this feature, additionally TTQ B1b1 (9F66, Offline Data Authentication for Online Authorizations supported) must be set.  |
| EMV_CTLS_ODO_SDA_VK | =12|  (Vel: y VFI n) VK2.2.3 only: Enable SDA for ODO  |
| EMV_CTLS_ODO_DDA_VK | =13|  (Vel: y VFI n) VK2.2.3 only: Enable fDDA for ODO  |
| EMV_CTLS_ODO_SDA_ERR_ONLINE_VK | =14|  (Vel: y VFI n) VK2.2.3 only: Outcome for ODO SDA error: 0 = Decline, 1 = Go online  |
| EMV_CTLS_ODO_DDA_ERR_ONLINE_VK | =15|  (Vel: y VFI n) VK2.2.3 only: Outcome for ODO fDDA error: 0 = Decline, 1 = Go online  |
| EMV_CTLS_OMIT_AUC_INT_CASH_VK | =16|  (Vel: y VFI n) Omit AUC "International Cash" check  |
| EMV_CTLS_OMIT_AUC_INT_CASHBACK_VK | =17|  (Vel: y VFI n) Omit AUC "International Cashback" check  |
| EMV_CTLS_OMIT_AUC_DOM_CASH_VK | =18|  (Vel: y VFI n) Omit AUC "Domestic Cash" check  |
| EMV_CTLS_OMIT_AUC_DOM_CASHBACK_VK | =19|  (Vel: y VFI n) Omit AUC "Domestic Cashback" check  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CASHBACK_AMOUNT_VK | =20|  (Vel: y VFI n) Set Cashback amount to zero for Cashback transactions. Workaround to allow Cashback transactions with Russian cards not supporting domestic Cashback  |
| EMV_CTLS_CASHBACK_TRANS_TYPE_VK9_VK | =21|  (Vel: y VFI n) Use Transaction Type 09 for cashback transactions. VCSP 2.2 mandates Transaction Type 00.  |
| EMV_CTLS_QUASI_CASH_VK | =22|  (Vel: y VFI n) Convert transaction type from '01' to '11' indicating VISA Quasi Cash. If supported by L2 kernel AUC checks for cash will be applied.  |
| EMV_CTLS_DO_NOT_CFG_9F21_TIME_VK | =23|  (Vel: y VFI n) Set Transaction Time tag 9F21 to "000000"  |
| EMV_CTLS_CARDREAD_GENAC1_ARQC_AK | =0|  B1b1: (Vel: y VFI: n) Card read transaction (e.g. refund): request ARQC in GENAC1, usually AAC is requested  |
| EMV_CTLS_TRANSACTION_TYPE_30_FOR_PREAUTH_AK | =1|  B1b2: (Vel: y VFI: n) Amex Pre-Authorization with transaction type 30 

 Use [EMV_ADK_TRAN_TYPE_AMEX_PREAUTH](group___t_r_a_n_s___t_y_p_e_s.md#define-emv-adk-tran-type-amex-preauth) for pre-authorization resp. reservation transactions 

 The modified transaction type is used towards card and put out in [EMV_CTLS_TRANSRES_STRUCT::T_9C_TransType](struct_e_m_v___c_t_l_s___t_r_a_n_s_r_e_s___s_t_r_u_c_t.md#variable-t-9c-transtype).  |

| EMV_CTLS_DISABLE_PIN_BELOW_CVM_CK | =6|  (Vel: y VFI: y) Do not ask for online PIN and Signature for transactions below CVM Limit when this was requested by card. This bit should be set for Credit / Quasi Credit AIDs according to Ref. "UPI QuickPass Implementation
                                        Guide for Acquirers v1.3.9": Terminals shall not ask for online PIN when all of below situations are met -QuickPass credit/Quasi credit cards are accepted, -Contactless transaction amount is below CVM limit of the terminal.  |

| EMV_CTLS_ON_DEVICE_CVM_SUPPORTED_RK | =6|  (Vel: y VFI: n) On-Device CVM (mobile CVM) supported  |
| EMV_CTLS_CVM_REQUIRED_RK | =7|  (Vel: y VFI: n) CVM required, transaction will fail in case card decision is "no CVM)  |
| EMV_CTLS_ISSUER_UPDATE_SUPPORTED_RK | =8|  (Vel: y VFI: n) Issuer script processing supported  |
| EMV_CTLS_STATUS_CHECK_ENABLE_WK | =0|  B1b1: Enable status check for one single unit of currency (one major currency unit, e.g. 1 is going online for status check). If TTQ 'online capable reader' is not set, 'Contactless Application Not Allowed' indicator will be set  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CHECK_ENABLE_SKIP_WK | =1|  B1b2: Enable zero check for zero amount transaction, Option 2: Set 'Contactless Application Not Allowed' indicator  |
| EMV_CTLS_ZERO_CHECK_ENABLE_ONLINE_WK | =2|  B1b3: Enable zero check for zero amount transaction, Option 1: Set TTQ 'Online cryptogram required', only possible if TTQ 'online capable reader' is set, otherwise 'Contactless Application Not Allowed' indicator is set  |
| EMV_CTLS_NO_CDCVM_WK | =3|  B1b4: Do not set TTQ B3b7  |
| EMV_CTLS_EXPLICIT_SELECT_DOM | =0|  B1b1: Try explicit select in case of non-EMV mode or PSE failed  |




scheme specific EMV flow capability bit numbers 


### enum EMVFlowOptionBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CTLS_VISA_WAVE | =0|  Support for Visa wave 

 for VFI reader or enabling Raptor VISA AP kernel (PDOL decision) 

 Info: VFI reader tag DF64, 1FF0 and others - This feature is not configurable per AID only global  |
| EMV_CTLS_OR_NONEMV_MARKET | =1|  Support for Amex EMV or NON EMV market 

 Map to Byte2 BIT1 of Contactless Kernel Options(1FF0) 

 Info: VFI reader tag 1FF0 - This feature is not configurable per AID only global  |
| EMV_CTLS_UI_SCHEME_DEFAULT | =2|  VFI reader only: Use reader's UI scheme "default", as standard "EMEA" is used.

 Visa Europe tests will fail if this is activated. But it's needed for display callback "L1 error" ([EMV_TXT_RETAP_SAME_L1](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txt-retap-same-l1))  |
| EMV_CTLS_AL_USE_TID | =3|  Use the TID as IFD Serial number. Background: If application can not provide IFD_Serial this can be used as replacement to have a unique value available (not for VFI-Reader).  |
| EMV_CTLS_LED_NON_VISA_EUROPE | =4|  Switch off Visa Europe work around for LED2. This option is like EMV_CTLS_UI_SCHEME_DEFAULT but for VERTEX.  |
| EMV_CTLS_LED_EP_OPTION_2 | =5|  Use LED scheme option 2 as defined in Entry Point spec [EMV BB]. Coloured LEDs similar to Visa Wave 2 (Visa Asia Pacific). For LED configuration see [EMV_CTLS_LED_ConfigDesign_Extended()](group___a_d_k___l_e_d.md#function-emv-ctls-led-configdesign-extended).  |
| EMV_CTLS_LED_INTERAC | =6|  Use LED blinking scheme for Interac (Canada)  |
| EMV_CTLS_FORWARD_VFI_FAIL | =7|  VFI Reader final scenario "Fail" is forwarded to the application by returning EMV_ADK_VFI_FAIL instead of per default EMV_ADK_AAC. Additionnally the ADK provides the SW12 in T_DF64_KernelDebugData[0]&[1], VFI Reader Error Code in T_DF64_KernelDebugData[3], and VFI Reader RF State Code in T_DF64_KernelDebugData[30]  |
| EMV_CTLS_DISABLE_DISCOVER_ZIP_CHECK | =8|  VFI Reader only: Disable the check according to D-PAS 1.0 Bulletin TAS-002 v1.0 which requires to consider the legacy Discover ZIP application as mandatory on any card/phone with the Discover/Diners D-PAS AID, and to reject the card if ZIP is not present  |




EMV terminal flow option bits 


### enum EMVChecksumOptionBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_INCLUDE_VERSION | =0|  default: NO --> For checksum only  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_TRANSACTION_LOG | =1|  default: YES --> De/activated per application  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_EXCEPTION_FILE | =2|  default: YES --> De/activated per application  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_FORCE_ONLINE | =3|  default: YES --> De/activated per application and by merchant  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_FORCE_ACCEPTANCE | =4|  default: YES --> De/activated per application and by merchant  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_ONL_DATA_CAPTURE | =5|  default: NO --> For checksum only --> application related decision  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_PSE | =6|  default: YES --> De/activated per transaction (EMV_Select)  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_ACCOUNT_TYPE | =7|  default: YES --> De/activated per application  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_ADVICES | =8|  default: NO --> Support of advices on host prot  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_CARDHOLDER_CONF | =9|  default: YES --> Cardholder Confirmation  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_PIN_BYPASS | =10|  default: NO --> PIN bypass  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_DEFAULT_TDOL | =11|  default: YES --> Default TDOL  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_BATCH_DATA_CAPTURE | =12|  default: YES --> Batch data capture  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_VOICE_REF_ISS | =13|  default: YES --> Issuer initiated referrals  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_SUPPORT_VOICE_REF_CARD | =14|  default: NO --> Card initiated referrals  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_MULTILANG_SUPPORT | =15|  default: YES since L2 7.0.2  |
| EMV_CT_CHECKSUM_PIN_BYPASS_ONCE | =16|  default: NO --> No subsequent PIN bypass when PIN bypass is active  |




EMV checksum options bits 


### enum EMVTransactionOptionBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_CBCK_APPLI_SEL | =0|  Callback function for customer application selection set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_AMOUNT_CONFIRMATION](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-amount-confirmation)) will be generated, if there are several application possible. 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks), [EMVTxn::setNoCardholderConfirm](structvfisdi_1_1_e_m_v_txn.md#function-setnocardholderconfirm).  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A | =1|  allow reservation type B even in case only type A is activated via configuration (see [EMVSpecialTransactions](classvfisdi_1_1_e_m_v_special_transactions.md) )  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_CBCK_DOMESTIC_APPS | =2|  Activate callback function for cross check if a domestic app remains in the candidate list or not ([SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_DOMESTIC_APPS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-domestic-apps))) 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_ADDALL | =3|  Add all PSE applications to the candidate list (Cartes Bancaires - France)  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_ADDBLO | =4|  Add blocked LOA applications to the candidate list (Interac - Canada)  |
| EMV_CT_NO_LONGEST_AID_MATCH | =5|  Do not perform the longest AID match (technical nonsense but needed for a few domestic certifcations)  |
| EMV_CT_ALLOW_BLOCKED | =6|  Allow blocked application to be processed (in Bank controlled terminals to enable script processing to unblock blocked cards)  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_REMOVEALL_BUT_EXCLUDED | =7|  Remove all candidates from terminal list except those which are contained in excluded AID list  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_PIN_BYPASS_NO_SUBSEQUENT | =8|  If PIN bypass is supported it usually is for subsequent PIN entries, too. However some ICS (even if minor change) may announce no subsequent PIN Bypass, so you can configure here  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_MULTIPLE_RANDOM_NUMBERS | =9|  Create a new value for 9F37, each time a random number is requested by the ICC. Per default one random number per transaction is generated. It is recommended to use multiple random numbers for security reasons.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_DCC_CALLBACK | =10|  DCC callback function set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_DCC](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-dcc)) will be invoked. 

 Callback is only invoked if DCC is allowed (trann amount was not yet used in PDOL or amount confirmation) resp. limit conversion is needed (transaction and configuration currency difference).

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) and [EMV_CT_DCC_CHECK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-dcc-check).  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_DCC_CALLBACK_ALWAYS | =11|  DCC callback funtion set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_DCC](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-dcc)) will be called always. 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) and [EMV_CT_DCC_CHECK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-dcc-check).  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_NO_FALLBACK_AFTER_CVM | =12|  Despite fallback after CVM allowed by appliction configuration stop transaction with card error. This is required in case of separate readers if mag. stripe has not been read prior to chip.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_AMOUNT_CONF | =13|  The callback for the amount confirmation will be generated, e.g. to be deactivated if terminal is unattended. 

 Invoking this callback depends on [EMV_CT_CONF_AMOUNT_PIN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-conf-amount-pin), [EMV_CT_REFUND_CONFIRM_AMOUNT](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-refund-confirm-amount), [EMV_CT_AMOUNT_CONFIRM_ON_SIGNATURE](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-amount-confirm-on-signature), [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks).  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_ENFORCE_PIN | =14|  Austrian (EPA) domestic feature: force PIN usage 

 In case no PIN entry was done during Cardholder Verification: EMV ADK will force online PIN entry.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_FALLBACK_GOODSERVICE | =15|  German domestic feature: Execute cash transaction with transaction type "Goods & Services" (in case application's background system does not support cash)  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_MERCHINFO_CALLBACK | =16|  The callback for the intermediate merchant information will be generated ([SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback)[EMV_CB_MERCHANT_INFO](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-merchant-info)) 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_RND_CALLBACK | =17|  Use own random number generator instead of OS one (not recommneded but for debug purposes useful), only for velocity kernel, see [EMV_CB_RANDOM](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-random) |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_HOTLST_LOG_CALLBACK | =18|  The callback for the transaction log / hotlist will be generated set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_CHECK_LOG_HOTLIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-check-log-hotlist)) 

 Depends on the AID parameters [EMV_CT_TRANSACTION_LOG](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-transaction-log) and [EMV_CT_BLACKLIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-blacklist), and on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_LOCAL_CHCK_CALLBACK | =19|  The callback for the domestic and local checks will be generated set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_DOMESTIC_APPS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-domestic-apps)) 

 Depends on the AID parameter [EMV_CT_DOMESTIC_CHECK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-domestic-check) and on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_CARDHINFO_CALLBACK | =20|  The callback for the intermediate cardholder information will be generated set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) ([EMV_CB_CARDHOLDER_INFO](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-cardholder-info)) 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-ms-return-callbacks) |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_EARLY_PIN_ENTRY | =21|  Early PIN entry. 

 PIN entry is done (by application) in parallel to steps "Read application data" and "Offline data authentication". 

 Depends on [EMV_CT_TXNOP_DELAYED_EARLY_PIN](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-delayed-early-pin). 

 If set: Application starts PIN entry after GPO, in callback "merchant info - start read
                                          record" ([SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback)[EMV_CB_MERCHANT_INFO](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-merchant-info) with #EMVMER_READ_APP_DATA) 

 If not set: Application starts PIN entry at callback "local checks" ([SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) with [EMV_CB_LOCAL_CHECKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-local-checks)).  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_DELAYED_EARLY_PIN | =22|  Delayed early PIN entry. 

 PIN entry is done (by application) after callback "local checks" ([SDIClient::setEMVCallback](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) with [EMV_CB_LOCAL_CHECKS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-local-checks)). 

 Precondition: [EMV_CT_TXNOP_EARLY_PIN_ENTRY](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-txnop-early-pin-entry) is active.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_KERNEL_PARSE_UNKNOWN_TLV | =23|  Let the kernel parse and store unknown [TLV](classvfisdi_1_1_t_l_v.md) templates so that unknown tags can be retrieved by EMV_CT_fetchTxnTags. Precondition is that those tags are configured in the additional tag store (Additional_Tags_CRD)  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_NO_UTF8 | =24|  Omit UTF-8 converted application labels in application selection callback [TAG_BF04_CBK_REDUCE_CAND](group___c_b_c_k___f_c_t___t_a_g_s.md#define-tag-bf04-cbk-reduce-cand) |
| EMV_CT_TRXOP_NO_UTF8 | =24|  Omit UTF-8 converted application labels in amount confirmation and PIN input callback functions ([TAG_BF02_CBK_AMOUNTCONF](group___c_b_c_k___f_c_t___t_a_g_s.md#define-tag-bf02-cbk-amountconf), [TAG_BF08_CBK_PIN](group___c_b_c_k___f_c_t___t_a_g_s.md#define-tag-bf08-cbk-pin))  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_TIP_AMOUNT_ZERO | =25|  Card holder confirmed zero amount within tip amount input dialog. In case of TIP setting DF22 position 4 = 3 the transaction shall not be made suitable for a tip follow-up.  |
| EMV_CT_TRXOP_NO_CHECK_BB_PADDING | =26|  Omit check for BB padding in card data authentication certificates - This check is obliged in some regions but not generally by EMVCo  |
| EMV_CT_TRXOP_NO_CHECK_DDLEN | =27|  Omit check if dynamic data length in card data authentication certificates is too big  |
| EMV_CT_ONL_OPTS_LAST_PIN_TRY | =32|  Host detected "last PIN try" for online PIN.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_PERFORM_ISS_ACQ_CVM | =33|  Currently not used! The callback for AcquirerCVM processing  |
| EMV_CT_TRXOP_WRITE_DS_OFFLINE_TXN | =35|  Write data storage data for offline transactions. Relevant only by Continue Online. When this option is set, EMV_CTLS_ContinueOnline will only write the DS data and will not perform the kernel online processing.  |
| EMV_CT_TXNOP_FORCE_TACIAC_DEFAULT | =36|  After Host Connection: Force TAC IAC Default processing even the host was reached, e.g. service provider host is available and returns valid AC but the issuer host was not reached fro cryptogram verification  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_WEEK_PRIORITY_APPS | =37|  Ignore priority applications that are not part of the terminal candidate list.  |
| EMV_CT_CUST_APPLI_SELECTION_PERFORMED | =38|  This is a possibility that allows the app to indicate that a customer application selection has been performed. If this is set, the callback / Reentrance for candidate selection will be even called if only one candidate is left. This is to inform the customer that the prior selected application was withdrawn from the candidate list after customer confirmation. In this special case a single candidate must not be selected automatically.  |
| EMV_CT_SELOP_DETECT_EMPTY_LIST | =39|  Without this bit in case of card error and in case of no common candidate [EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-fallback) is returned for backwards compatibility. If enabled, the second case results in return code [EMV_STATUS_TXN_EMPTY_LIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-txn-empty-list).  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_SUPPRESS_ERRMSGBEEP | =0|  Suppress beep on error message display  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_REPEAT_L1 | =1|  TXN repeated because of L1 error (same txn is started a 2nd time)  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_DOMESTIC_KERNEL | =2|  skip local kernel processing for this transaction even if configured  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_GLOBAL | =3|  skip global EMV processing for this transaction even if configured  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_PP_TORNTXN_RESET | =4|  reset the torn transaction store if a PayPass card is presented  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_AK_DELAYED_AUTH | =5|  Amex delayed autorization (amex 3.1 and above), set this bit if after an Amex txn the host is not reachable (allows a retap with AAC or TC decision)  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_REMOVEALL_BUT_EXCLUDED | =7|  B1b8: Remove all candidates from terminal list except those which are contained in excluded AID list  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_CANDLIST_CALLBACK | =8|  common candidate list of terminal and card reported, see [EMV_CB_MODIFY_CANDIDATES](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-modify-candidates) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_APPSELECTED_CALLBACK | =9|  callback after the final select, only available for velocity kernel, see [EMV_CB_APP_SELECTED](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-app-selected) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_BUL12 | =10|  SU Bulletin 12 NOT supported (Velocitoy Entrypoint _NOT_ EMVEP_CFG_BUL12)  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_LONGEST_AID_MATCH | =12|  Do not perform the longest AID match (technical nonsense but needed for a few domestic certifcations)  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_SPURIOUS_CARD_DETECT | =13|  Try to avoid spurious card detections on ADK level (workaround for L1 issues, code provided by platform team)  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_PAN_RETRIEVE_DEF | =14|  PayPass: Do NOT Use default configuration for PAN Retrieval Transactions but configured values. 

 For all other schemes EMV ADK does anyhow use configured values for PAN retrieval transactions. 

 Not yet supported for VFI reader.  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_RND_CALLBACK | =15|  Use own random number generator instead of OS one (not recommneded but for debug purposes useful), only supported for velocity kernel, see [EMV_CB_RANDOM](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-random) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_OMIT_CHECKSUM_CHECK | =16|  VFI-Reader: Dont calculate checksums of configuration files 

 Only effective on [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_STOP_ON_CHKSUM_DIFF | =17|  VFI-Reader: abort transaction when checksums of configuration files changed 

 Only effective on [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_NO_AMOUNT_PRECHECK | =19|  Disable the amount precheck --> even tap card is requested (Setup successful) if the txn amount is higher than the highest transaction limit of any AID / kernel. --> This results in terminate or fallabck later on  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_L1_ERROR_CALLBACK | =20|  Enable notification callback for display "Error, try again" ([EMV_TXT_RETAP_SAME_L1](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txt-retap-same-l1)) in case of L1 error and "Use 1 card only" ([EMV_TXT_2_CARDS_IN_FIELD](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txt-2-cards-in-field)) in case 2 cards are detected 

 Precondition: UI scheme "default" is set, use [EMV_CTLS_UI_SCHEME_DEFAULT](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-ui-scheme-default) |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_SETUP_WAIT_FOR_ERROR | =21|  VFI-Reader: [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) waits 10 ms for a negative answer from VFI-Reader so in case of VFI-Reader having problems, this is already detected in [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) rather than in [EMV_CTLS_ContinueOffline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-continueoffline).  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_WEEK_PRIORITY_APPS | =22|  Ignore priority applications that are not part of the terminal candidate list  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_PRELOAD_TRANSACTION | =23|  Preload feature: perform preliminary process and prepare database for payment without starting the transaction. Required for VAS processing using NFC ADK on VFI reader.  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_KEEP_MULTIPLE_KERNEL | =24|  After Final Select keep all AID-kernel combinations for the selected AID  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_TIP_AMOUNT_ZERO | =25|  Card holder confirmed zero amount within tip amount input dialog. In case of TIP setting DF22 position 4 = 3 the the transaction shall not be made suitable for a tip follow-up.  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_SILENT_ON_EMPTY_LIST | =26|  In case of empty candidate list (return code [EMV_STATUS_TXN_EMPTY_LIST](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-txn-empty-list)) suppress error tone and LED processing (LEDs off after 750ms).  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_CVM_REQUIRED | =27|  Force CVM for this transaction due to a special business use case. Basically implemented by internally setting the CVM required limits to zero.  |
| EMV_CTLS_TXNOP_LONG_TAP_TIMER | =28|  Set timer for Present And Hold timeout function according JCB Contactless IC Terminal Specification with value of Removal Timeout unless 0. In case of timeout contactless field is powered-off, "Card Read OK" display request is sent and light and sound indicators are triggered. For details please see [Present And Hold Transaction ("Long Tap")] |




EMV transaction option bits 


### enum EMVTransactionStepBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_CANDIDATE_LIST | =0|  return for selecting the candidate on application level  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_AFTER_GPO | =1|  return after finishing GPO  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_AFTER_READ_RECORD | =2|  return after finishing ReadRecords  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_AFTER_DATA_AUTH | =3|  return after finishing Data Authentication  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_FOR_CVM_PROCESS | =4|  for each selected CV PIN method the control is given to the application to handle it  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_FOR_CVM_FINISH | =5|  CV finished  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_AFTER_RISK_MANGEMENT | =7|  return after finishing the terminal risk management (before 1st GAC)  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_CAND_LIST_PREPROC | =8|  return once the candidate list is known to manipulate the list  |
| EMV_CT_RETURN_CAND_LIST_SKIP | =9|  Candidate list building by calling application.  |
| EMV_CT_MS_ADD_TO_HOTLIST | =16|  If Set: The card of this txn will be added to the hotlist (processed after ReadRecords)  |
| EMV_CT_MS_DECLINE_AAC | =17|  If Set: The transaction will be declined with requesting an AAC  |
| EMV_CT_MS_ABORT_TXN | =18|  If Set: The transaction will be terminated immediately  |
| EMV_CT_MS_PIN_BYPASS | =19|  If Set: Customer or Merchant bypassed PIN entry  |
| EMV_CT_MS_CUST_CVM_OK | =20|  If Set: Customer CVM method success  |
| EMV_CT_MS_PINPAD_NOTPRESENT | =21|  If Set: external PINPad was not detected for PIN processing  |
| EMV_CT_MS_PINICC_STOP | =22|  If Set: ICC stopped working during PIN processing  |
| EMV_CT_MS_RETURN_CALLBACKS | =23|  If Set: All callbacks are disabled completely, otherwise they are used as configured in the parameter set  |




EMV transaction step bits 


### enum EMVDomesticOptionBits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_DOM_AUSTRIAN_NGV | =0|  Continue transaction as Austrian Non Guaranteed Payment.  |
| EMV_DOM_TXN_INTERCEPT | =1|  Intercept transaction. Context will remain. Repetition transaction must be started with [EMV_TXN_REPEAT_TXN_INTERCEPT](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-repeat-txn-intercept).  |
| EMV_DOM_ABORT_NO_TEXT | =2|  if the EMV callback set by [SDIClient::setEMVCallback()](group__sdicallback.md#function-setemvcallback) with ([EMV_CB_DOMESTIC_APPS](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-cb-domestic-apps)) returns `FALSE` and `uc_manipulation` != [EMV_STATUS_AAC](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-aac): Don't display texts [EMV_TXT_PROCESSING_ERROR](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txt-processing-error) and [EMV_TXT_REMOVE_CARD](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txt-remove-card)

 Otherwise not effective  |
| EMV_DOM_TIP_OFF | =3|  convert a tip capable transaction back to sale transaction (used for countries where tip with signature is done outside the scope of EMV and returns the txn to a normal sale transaction)  |




domestic option bits

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| OK | =0|  no error  |
| FAIL | =-1|  generic error  |

### enum InputType

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| INPUT_ZIP | =1|  input ZIP code (4-6 digits)  |
| INPUT_CVV | =2|  input card verification code (3-4 digits)  |
| INPUT_BIRTHDAY | =3|  input date of birth ( 8 digits, MMDDYYYY)  |
| INPUT_SSN | =4|  input social security number (SSN) (9 digits)  |
| INPUT_SSN_LAST_4 | =5|  input last 4 digits of SSN  |
| VERIFY_ZIP | =6|  verify ZIP code (4-6 digits)  |
| VERIFY_CVV | =7|  verify card verification code (3-4 digits)  |
| VERIFY_BIRTHDAY | =8|  verify date of birth ( 8 digits, MMDDYYYY)  |
| VERIFY_SSN | =9|  verify social security number (SSN) (9 digits)  |
| VERIFY_SSN_LAST_4 | =10|  verify last 4 digits of SSN  |
| INPUT_TIP_AMOUNT | =11|  input tip amount  |
| INPUT_TIP_PERCENT | =12|  input tip percentage  |
| INPUT_CASHBACK_AMOUNT | =13|  input cashback amount  |
| INPUT_TIP_AMOUNT_DISPLAY | =14|  input tip amount with displaying the payment amount  |
| INPUT_EMAIL | =15|  input email address  |
| INPUT_PHONE | =16|  input phone number  |
| INPUT_INSTALLMENTS | =17|  input number of installments  |

### enum EMVOptions

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_OPT_BASE_INIT | =0x00000001|  base init: set options and register callback, but do not allocate memory  |
| EMV_OPT_L1_DUMP | =0x00000002|   |
| EMV_OPT_AUTO_RETAP | =0x00000004|  Do NOT handle retaps as two separate transactions but handle retaps internally and fire message events only to the app (TAG_BF14_CBK_TEXT_DISPLAY), the retap returncodes (like EMV_ADK_TXN_CTLS_MOBILE) will not appear in this case but processing is handled on ADK level.  Detailed explanation:  VFI-Reader: The VFI-reader in general manges the retap for a mobile internally, ALWAYS. There is no chance for the ADK hand over the retap for a moblie transaction to the application. Therefore the EMV_ADK_TXN_CTLS_MOBILE does NEVER appear with VRFI-Reader.  Velocity: On velovcity the kernel is NEVER handling the retap internally. So the ADK can hand it over to the application. Then you would receive EMV_ADK_TXN_CTLS_MOBILE. For compatibility reasons with the VFI-Reader we have introduced that the ADK is handling the mobile retap optionally. This is configurable with this parameter. If you configure this, then also the EMV_ADK_TXN_CTLS_MOBILE is NEVER returned to the application. If you do not configure it this returncode will appear.  Only if internal handling of the Velocity or the VFI-Reader takes place, the BF14 callback is issued to allow the application to display something. If the configuration is in that way that the app wants to handle the mobile retap according to its needs, then the BF14 is NEVER invoked. This is mutually exclusive.  |
| EMV_OPT_CONFIG_MODE | =0x00000008|  configuration is only written to files upon ExitFramework and ApplyConfiguration instead of written upon each configuration function -> performance improvement  |
| EMV_OPT_USE_DEF_VT_CAPK | =0x00000010|  Use "EMV_CTLS_Keys.xml" for the CAPKeys of ALL virtual terminals. This option is to be set by the initialization of the virtual terminal 0 only. Once set this feature applies to all virtual terminals.  |
| EMV_OPT_DELETE_ALL | =0x00000020|  delete all existing configuration files using the same virtual terminal  |
| EMV_OPT_USE_VFI | =0x00000040|  Decrecated  |
| EMV_OPT_USE_VERTEX | =0x00000080|  Decrecated  |
| EMV_OPT_TRACE | =0x00000100|  switch on EMV trace  |
| EMV_OPT_TRACE_CLT | =0x00000200|  switch on client trace  |
| EMV_OPT_LED_CBK_EXT | =0x00000400|  request external LED display. Per default the LEDs are displayed in the configured region by using the GUI ADK. It is highly recommended to use this default for speed reasons. It is possible to offer a callback so that LEDs can be managed on apps side by using this callback (TAG_BF10_CTLS_CBK_LEDS).  |
| EMV_OPT_TRACE_SYSLOG | =0x00000800|  use syslog instead of callback for trace. Not possible for Verix.  |
| EMV_OPT_LED_VFI_INT | =0x00001000|  VFI Reader only: request internal LED display. If set, LED handling is done internally by the VFI Reader. If not set, LED display depends on EMV_CTLS_INIT_OPT_LED_CBK_EXT.  |
| EMV_OPT_VFI_BUZZER_ADK | =0x00004000|  VFI Reader only: Buzzer is not done by VFI reader, ADK takes over the beeps. see also [EMV_CTLS_TERMDATA_STRUCT::BeepVolume](struct_e_m_v___c_t_l_s___t_e_r_m_d_a_t_a___s_t_r_u_c_t.md#variable-beepvolume).  |
| EMV_OPT_CALC_CHKSUM | =0x00010000|  Calculate checksums of configuration files, may lead to setting of result bit EMV_CTLS_INIT_RES_CHKSUM_DIFF.  |
| EMV_OPT_NEW_CFG_INTF | =0x00020000|   |
| EMV_OPT_BEEP_CBK_EXT | =0x00040000|  Activate beeper callback (TAG_BF19_CTLS_CBK_BEEP). Per default beeper is controlled by EMV ADK.  |
| EMV_OPT_TRACE_ADK_LOG | =0x00080000|  use ADK-LOG instead of callback for trace  |
| EMV_OPT_TIMINGS | =0x00100000|  measure card and terminal performance. Note: For this feature other trace output is switched off  |
| EMV_OPT_SHARED_CONFIG | =0x00200000|  On VOS/VOS2 use /mnt/flash/etc/config/adkemv for persistence instead of $HOME/flash. NOTE: Only tje processes very first EMV_CTLS_Init_Framework decides the shared config mode.  |
| EMV_OPT_EPP_MASTER | =0x00400000|  Generate a Configuration Id for every configuration change at time of persisting. Generate a checksum for every persistence file to be aware of changes via file system. The configuration id is specific to a Virtual Terminal and returned on Init Framework and when the configuration is stored to the file system. It is seen on serial interface only.  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_1 | =0x01000000|  virtual terminal 1: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_2 | =0x02000000|  virtual terminal 2: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_3 | =0x03000000|  virtual terminal 3: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_4 | =0x04000000|  virtual terminal 4: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_5 | =0x05000000|  virtual terminal 5: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_6 | =0x06000000|  virtual terminal 6: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_7 | =0x07000000|  virtual terminal 7: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_8 | =0x08000000|  virtual terminal 8: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_9 | =0x09000000|  virtual terminal 9: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_10 | =0x0A000000|  virtual terminal 10: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_11 | =0x0B000000|  virtual terminal 11: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_12 | =0x0C000000|  virtual terminal 12: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_13 | =0x0D000000|  virtual terminal 13: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_14 | =0x0E000000|  virtual terminal 14: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_15 | =0x0F000000|  virtual terminal 15: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_16 | =0x10000000|  virtual terminal 16: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_17 | =0x11000000|  virtual terminal 17: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_18 | =0x12000000|  virtual terminal 18: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_19 | =0x13000000|  virtual terminal 19: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |
| EMV_OPT_VIRT_20 | =0x14000000|  virtual terminal 20: configuration and transaction not done with the standard terminal but virtual terminal No X  |




EMV initialization options 


### enum EMVStatus

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_STATUS_OK | =0x00| Function successful, no error.   |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_START | =0xA0|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return start reserved codes  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_CANDIDATE | =0xA1|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return application selection  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_READREC | =0xA2|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return read records  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_DATAAUTH | =0xA3|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return data authentication  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_ONL_PIN | =0xA4|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for online PIN entry  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_OFFL_PIN | =0xA5|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for offline PIN entry  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_PLAIN_PIN | =0xA6|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for plaintext PIN entry  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_CVM_END | =0xA7|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return cardholder verification  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_RISK_MAN | =0xA8|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return riskmanagement  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_CUST_CVM | =0xA9|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for customCVM method  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_APPS_PREPROC | =0xAA|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for candidate list manipulation  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_AFTER_GPO | =0xAB|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return for return after GPO  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_BUILD_LIST | =0xAC|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return before terminal candidate list build  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_REQ_END | =0xAF|  CT Reentrance mode: Application requested return end of reserved codes  |
| EMV_STATUS_TIMEOUT | =0xC8|  Timeout  |
| EMV_STATUS_MAX_CFG_NUMBER_EXCEEDED | =0xC9|  CTLS: Number of keys uploaded to VFI Reader exceeded (appears when number of keys more than 99, all next keys are ignored)  |
| EMV_STATUS_VFI_FAIL | =0xCA|  VFI Reader "Fail" result. Transaction is terminated and application should decide about the final outcome (decline, fallback, try another card, etc...) based on the VFI Reader response data items (Error Code - SW1 - SW2 - RF State Code). This is returned only with VFI Reader and only if the Terminal Flow Option INPUT_CTLS_TRM_FLOWOPT_FORWARD_VFI_FAIL is set, otherwise EMV_STATUS_AAC is returned per default.  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_OFFLINE_PIN | =0xCB|  Transaction to be continued after PIN input for girocard (German debit card) Offline PIN CVM  |
| EMV_STATUS_NOT_ACCEPTED | =0xCC|  Transaction / Payment type not accepted  |
| EMV_STATUS_CANCELLED | =0xCD|  Transaction was cancelled by [EMV_CTLS_Break()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-break) |
| EMV_STATUS_CARD_LOG_LOG_OK | =0xCE|  Return code for successful read of cards transaction log (currently qPBOC only)  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_LOW_BATTERY | =0xCF|  Return code for EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction indicating mobile device's battery too low for contactless transaction.  |
| EMV_STATUS_NOT_ALLOWED_WRONG_CFG_INTF | =0xD0|  CTLS: The function is not allowed when using this config interface  |
| EMV_STATUS_VIRTTERMMAP_WRONG_INIT | =0xD1|   |
| EMV_STATUS_TOO_MANY_TAPS | =0xD2|   |
| EMV_STATUS_CAN_NOT_PROCESS | =0xD3|   |
| EMV_STATUS_USE_ANOTHER_CTLS_CARD | =0xD4|  CTLS: advice the customer to use another CTLS card (will appear only if the CTLS kernel is configured in that way that Contact Chip is not supported)  |
| EMV_STATUS_USE_OTHER_TERMINAL | =0xD5|  CTLS: advice the merchant to use another terminal to process the transaction (Interac spec requirement)  |
| EMV_STATUS_SCRIPT_PROCESSING_COMPLETE | =0xD6|  CTLS: explicit script processing completed (CTLS, e.g. Discover DPAS)  |
| EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK_CHIP_ONLY | =0xD7|  CTLS: Fallback to chip (CTLS), no msr allowed  |
| EMV_STATUS_READER_CMD_NOT_ALLOWED | =0xD8|  VFI-Reader: Returned by [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) and [EMV_CTLS_ContinueOffline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-continueoffline) if VFI-Reader responds to "Activate Transaction" with "Command not allowed". This happens if VFI-Reader has not yet finished last transaction, e.g. is still waiting for ContinueOnline.  |
| EMV_STATUS_NOT_ALLOWED | =0xD9|  Parallel function call not allowed  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_NOT_AVAILABLE | =0xDA|  CTLS not present on hardware per OS information  |
| EMV_STATUS_USR_BCKSPC_KEY_PRESSED | =0xDB|  Application requested return for E_USR_BACKSPACE_KEY_PRESSED, not used anymore  |
| EMV_STATUS_CEILING_LIMIT | =0xDC|  CTLS: amount is above the ceiling limit for CTLS (either terminal ceiling limit or highest scheme ceiling limit)  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_RETAP_SAME | =0xDD|  CTLS: start over with re-tapping the same card (deactivation/activation/start txn)  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_DOMESTIC_APP | =0xDE|  CTLS: Domestic Application Kernel selected  |
| EMV_STATUS_NO_CARD | =0xDF|  CTLS: No card processing so far  |
| EMV_STATUS_NOAPP | =0xE0|  CT: Return code if application not found by [EMV_CT_CheckSupportedAID()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ct-checksupportedaid).

 CTLS: Empty terminal candidate list (e.g. all application's ceiling limits exceeded) at [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction).  |
| EMV_STATUS_NO_EXEC | =0xE1|  CT & CTLS: not executable  |
| EMV_STATUS_ARQC | =0xE2|  CT & CTLS: Transaction must be performed online  |
| EMV_STATUS_TC | =0xE3|  CT & CTLS: Transaction performed (offline / online)  |
| EMV_STATUS_AAC | =0xE4|  CT & CTLS: Transaction declined  |
| EMV_STATUS_AAR | =0xE5|  CT: Transaction cancellation (former "card referral"), not used anymore  |
| EMV_STATUS_PARAM | =0xE6|  CT & CTLS: Parameter error (wrong parameter was passed to the function)  |
| EMV_STATUS_CARDERR | =0xE7|  CT & CTLS: Proprietary card error (actually converted to [EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-fallback))  |
| EMV_STATUS_BADAPP | =0xE8|  CT: Repeat EMV_Select function call-up because selected application on the proprietary card is erroneous. The currently selected application must be transferred (not NO_APPLI) -> this leads to new application selection but the candidate list is not reconstructed.  |
| EMV_STATUS_CVM | =0xE9|  CT: User abort during PIN input (cancel button, timeout, card removed)  |
| EMV_STATUS_ABORT | =0xEA|  On transaction function it means that current transaction must be aborted.

 On configuration function it represents "failed".  |
| EMV_STATUS_CARD_BLOCKED | =0xEB|  CT & CTLS: Blocked card, regional dependent if fallback to magstripe should be done  |
| EMV_STATUS_CARDERR_FORMAT | =0xEC|  Card error e.g. erroneous [TLV](classvfisdi_1_1_t_l_v.md) coding, incorrect data -> no transaction cancellation  |
| EMV_STATUS_INTERNAL | =0xED|  CT & CTLS: e.g. erroneous communication to PINPad, internal error, not (completely) initialized (function not allowed due to [EMV_CT_Init_Framework()](group___f_u_n_c___i_n_i_t.md#define-emv-ct-init-framework) with `[EMV_CT_INIT_OPT_BASE_INIT()](group___c_t_i_n_i_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-emv-ct-init-opt-base-init)`
[EMV_CTLS_Init_Framework()](group___f_u_n_c___i_n_i_t.md#define-emv-ctls-init-framework) with `[EMV_CTLS_INIT_OPT_BASE_INIT()](group___c_l_i_n_i_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-emv-ctls-init-opt-base-init)` )  |
| EMV_STATUS_ONLINE_PIN_RETRY | =0xEE|  CT: Online PIN reentered (PIN check).
[EMV_CT_ContinueOnline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ct-continueonline)/EMV_CTLS_ContinueOnline() will return this value in the following scenario: Online PIN was entered. Host returned "PIN wrong".

 Calling application must contact host again. And afterwards call [EMV_CT_ContinueOnline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ct-continueonline) / [EMV_CTLS_ContinueOnline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-continueonline) once again.  |
| EMV_STATUS_SAVE_ERROR | =0xEF|  Writing config files failed. ANSI C functions fopen(), fwrite(), or fclose() gave back error. Make sure that file access rights are setup correctly.  |
| EMV_STATUS_APP_BLOCKED | =0xF0|  Application blocked: AID evaluation at fallback, no global fallback because it is not allowed for this special blocked application  |
| EMV_STATUS_READ_ERROR | =0xF1|  Error while reading EMV configuration  |
| EMV_STATUS_ERR_HSM | =0xF2|  E.g. erroneous communication to PINPad, internal error, not used anymore  |
| EMV_STATUS_TLV_BUILD_ERR | =0xF3|  CT & CTLS: Error in [TLV](classvfisdi_1_1_t_l_v.md) data object = internal error  |
| EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK | =0xF4|  CT & CTLS: Fallback to chip/msr (for CTLS) respectively magstripe (for CT) must be done  |
| EMV_STATUS_ONL_PIN_REPEAT | =0xF5|  CT: wrong Online-PIN, repeat transaction (reduced) beginning with [EMV_CT_StartTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ct-starttransaction) / [EMV_CTLS_SetupTransaction()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-setuptransaction) |
| EMV_STATUS_MAND_ELEM_MISSING | =0xF6|  CT: mandatory ([TLV](classvfisdi_1_1_t_l_v.md)) element missing (EMV-configuration), not used anymore  |
| EMV_STATUS_INVALID_TERM_CAP | =0xF7|  CT & CTLS: invalid terminal capabilities (EMV-configuration), not used anymore  |
| EMV_STATUS_REFERRAL | =0xF8|  CT: a referral of the application decides if the TXN is approved or not  |
| EMV_STATUS_2_CTLS_CARDS | =0xF9|  CTLS: 2 CTLS cards in the field detected. If this is reported after a call to ContinueOffline 2 cards have been detected in the field. The transaction is terminated in this case and must be restarted with a new call of SetupTransaction. This is mandatory for the VFI-Reader ADK and optional (but works as well) for teh Velocity/VERTX based ADK.  |
| EMV_STATUS_TXN_CTLS_L1_ERR | =0xFA|  CTLS: level 1 problem, retap necessary  |
| EMV_STATUS_TXN_CTLS_MOBILE | =0xFB|  CTLS: mobile device, retap necessary  |
| EMV_STATUS_TXN_EMPTY_LIST | =0xFC|  CTLS: empty candidate list. The application shall display "please use
                                      other interface" and (depending on regional market requirements) additionally "or tap another card" CT & CTLS: Empty candidate List = no common application between card and terminal. For CT usually [EMV_STATUS_FALLBACK](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-status-fallback) is returned in any case, card error and empty list. If the caller needs to distinguish these cases, she has to enable this return code via EMVConf::setTransactionOptions() bit EMV_CT_SELOP_DETECT_EMPTY_LIST  |
| EMV_STATUS_TXN_CTLS_EMV_USE_OTHER_CARD | =0xFD|  CTLS: insert, swipe or try another card  |
| EMV_STATUS_CTLS_DOMESTIC_ONLY_NOT_READABLE | =0xFE|  CTLS: domestic not readable (no AID and EMV not configured)  |
| EMV_STATUS_CONTINUE | =0xFF|  CT & CTLS: Transaction can be continued (e.g. CTLS Commit)  |

options for emvCtUpdateTxnTags 


### enum EMVFetchOptions

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_FETCH_NO_EMPTY | =0x01|  In case no data is found for a given [TLV](classvfisdi_1_1_t_l_v.md) tag: don't include this tag in the output.  |
| EMV_FETCH_KERNEL | =0x02|  Search tags only in kernel database, excluding kernel private tags ("readHypTag"). Data originated from kernel, ICC and [EMV_CT_APPLIDATA_STRUCT::Additional_Tags_TRM](struct_e_m_v___c_t___a_p_p_l_i_d_a_t_a___s_t_r_u_c_t.md#variable-additional-tags-trm) can be found. To be used in case of double definition of tags.  |
| EMV_FETCH_ADK | =0x04|  Search tags only in the ADK configuration database. Data originated from EMV_CT_APPLIDATA_TYPE and [EMV_CT_TERMDATA_STRUCT](struct_e_m_v___c_t___t_e_r_m_d_a_t_a___s_t_r_u_c_t.md) can be found. To be used in case of double definition of tags.  |
| EMV_FETCH_KERNEL_PRV | =0x08|  Search tags only in kernel private database ("readHypTag").  |

### enum EMVCtReaderOptions

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CT_CUSTOMER | =0x00|  bit 1,2 used for reader selection: Customer Card Slot  |
| EMV_CT_SAM_1 | =0x01|  bit 1,2 used for reader selection: SAM1  |
| EMV_CT_SAM_2 | =0x02|  bit 1,2 used for reader selection: SAM2  |
| EMV_CT_SAM_3 | =EMV_CT_SAM_1\|EMV_CT_SAM_2|  bit 1,2 used for reader selection: SAM3  |
| EMV_CT_TRY_PPS | =0x04|  Try to increase the baudrate by using PPS.  |
| EMV_CT_SKIP_ATR | =0x08|  Skip ATR reading, not included in response.  |
| EMV_CT_TRY_PPS_EPA | =0x10|  PPS handling for Austrian Maestro Cards.  |
| EMV_CT_WARMRESET | =0x20|  Warm Reset to ICC (Cold reset must have been applied before)  |
| EMV_CT_SAM_EMV_MODE | =0x40|  SAMs are reset in mode ISO 7816 per default, use this bit to switch to EMV 311 (for SAMs only)  |
| EMV_CT_DETECT_WRONG_ATR | =0x40|  Distinguish between wrong ATR and card wrong side/no chip and return applicable return value (for customer slot only)  |
| EMV_CT_CARD_CLASS_B_3V | =0x80|  For class B (3V) cards  |
| EMV_CT_ID0_ISO_MODE | =0x80|  The customer card (ID 0) is reset in mode EMV per default, use this bit to switch to ISO 7816 (for ID0 only)  |




SDI CT card reader options (bit mask) 


### enum EMVCtlsReaderOptions

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_CTLS_RFU_1 | =0x01|  reserved for probable reader number  |
| EMV_CTLS_RESET_KEEP_FIELD_ON | =0x02|  (Vel: y VFI: n) [EMV_CTLS_SmartReset()](group___f_u_n_c___i_c_c.md#function-emv-ctls-smartreset) ucOptions: Do not switch off RF field when no card was detected. CAUTION: This results in higher power consumption and might cause overheating problems.  |
| EMV_CTLS_RFU_3 | =0x04|  had been EMV_CTLS_SPURIOUS_DETECT before which was deprecated since August 2020  |
| EMV_CTLS_SPURIOUS_DETECT | =0x04|   |
| EMV_CTLS_EMV_COMPLIANT | =0x08|  (Vel: y VFI: n) [EMV_CTLS_SmartReset()](group___f_u_n_c___i_c_c.md#function-emv-ctls-smartreset) ucOptions: force EMV compliancy during card detection (e.g. MiFare detection deactivated), no detection of hybrid cards (e.g. EMV+MiFare), no UID detection. This feature is mutually exclusive with EMV_CTLS_RESET_NO_EMV.  |
| EMV_CTLS_RESET_NO_EMV | =0x10|  (Vel: y VFI: n) [EMV_CTLS_SmartReset()](group___f_u_n_c___i_c_c.md#function-emv-ctls-smartreset) ucOptions: Card detection without EMV compliancy (EMV cards are also detected, but timing is different). This feature is mutually exclusive with EMV_CTLS_EMV_COMPLIANT.  |
| EMV_CTLS_RESET_PICC_OPEN_ONLY | =0x20|   |
| EMV_CTLS_SKIP_FIELD_ON | =0x40|  (Vel: n VFI: y) [EMV_CTLS_SmartReset()](group___f_u_n_c___i_c_c.md#function-emv-ctls-smartreset) ucOptions: Tell VFI Reader to consider RF Field is already turned on by NFC ADK.  |
| EMV_CTLS_OPEN_READER | =EMV_CTLS_RESET_PICC_OPEN_ONLY|  (Vel: y VFI: n) option for EMV_CTLS_SmartPowerOff, initialise CTLS reader. Use in combination [EMV_CTLS_OPEN_READER](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-open-reader) for re-open.  |
| EMV_CTLS_CLOSE_READER | =0x40|  (Vel: y VFI: n) option for EMV_CTLS_SmartPowerOff, close CTLS reader. Use in combination [EMV_CTLS_OPEN_READER](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ctls-open-reader) for re-open.  |
| EMV_CTLS_DETECT_REMOVAL | =0x80|  (Vel: y VFI: n) option for EMV_CTLS_SmartPowerOff, start removal detection background task  |




SDI CTLS card reader options (bit mask) 


### enum EMVLEDMode

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_LED_MODE_OFF | =0x00|  switching LEDs must be done by the application  |
| EMV_LED_MODE_API | =0x01|  switching LEDs must be done by the API function [EMV_CTLS_LED()](group___a_d_k___l_e_d.md#function-emv-ctls-led) |
| EMV_LED_MODE_EMV | =0x02|  switching LEDs is done by EMV framework on its own (this is the initial mode)  |

| EMV_CB_DCC | 0xBF07|  Dynamic currency conversion (DCC)  |
| EMV_CB_PIN | 0xBF08|  PIN Input  |
| EMV_CB_CARDHOLDER_INFO | 0xBF09|  A text information has to be displayed to the cardholder  |

| EMV_CB_APP_SELECTED | 0xBF0C|  Signals that application is selected  |
| EMV_CB_DATA_EXCHANGE | 0xBF0E|  Callback for PP3 DataExchange  |
| EMV_CB_EXIT_THREAD | 0xBF0F|  Signals the stop of the "notification callback thread", no reply is sent  |

| EMV_CB_MODIFY_CANDIDATES | 0xBF12|  Modify candidate list  |
| EMV_CB_RANDOM | 0xBF13|  Random number provided by the calling application  |
| EMV_CB_TEXT_DISPLAY | 0xBF14|  Text display, no reply is sent  |
| EMV_CB_CARD_TAPPED | 0xBF15|  Notification that a card was detected, no reply is sent  |
| EMV_CB_SERVICE_SHORTLIST | 0xBF16|  RuPay callback before GPO  |
| EMV_CB_SERVICE_FOR_GENAC | 0xBF17|  RuPay callback before Generate AC  |
| EMV_CB_PURE_GET_PUT_DATA | 0xBF18|  Gemalto/Pure callback to provide GET DATA and/or PUT DATA input  |
| EMV_CB_BEEP | 0xBF19|  Application shall sound the buzzer, no reply is sent  |

| EMV_TXT_2_CARDS_IN_FIELD | =0x17| CTLS only: 2 card detected in the field    Only sent in case [CLTRXOP_L1_ERROR_CALLBACK()]() is activated.   |
| EMV_TXT_CARD_READ_COMPLETE | =0x18| CTLS only: waiting for Card Removal in the ADK , App should display Card Read Complete, Remove Card    Only sent in case CTLS_WAIT_CARD_REMOVAL_END() in application flow capabilties is activated.   |

### enum EMVSpecialReservation

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_RESERVATION_NO | =0|  reservation forbidden  |
| EMV_RESERVATION_A | =1|  reservation variant a (without partial reversal) allowed, no amount increment (Reservierung-Erhoehung) 

 according to EMVConf::setTransactionType(): [EMV_TXN_INIT_RESERVATION_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-init-reservation-a)

 for exception case see [EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-selop-reserv-allow-b-on-a) |
| EMV_RESERVATION_A_PLUS | =2|  reservation variant a (without partial reversal) allowed, amount increment (Reservierung-Erhoehung) allowed 

 according to EMVConf::setTransactionType(): [EMV_TXN_INIT_RESERVATION_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-init-reservation-a) and [EMV_TXN_INCREMENT_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-increment-a)

 for exception case see [EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-selop-reserv-allow-b-on-a) |
| EMV_RESERVATION_B | =3|  reservation variant b (with partial reversal) allowed, no amount increment (Reservierung-Erhoehung) 

 according to EMVConf::setTransactionType(): [EMV_TXN_INIT_RESERVATION_B](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-init-reservation-b)

 for exception case see [EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-selop-reserv-allow-b-on-a) |
| EMV_RESERVATION_B_PLUS | =4|  reservation variant b (with partial reversal) allowed, amount increment (Reservierung-Erhoehung) allowed 

 according to EMVConf::setTransactionType(): [EMV_TXN_INIT_RESERVATION_B](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-init-reservation-b) and [EMV_TXN_INCREMENT_B](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-increment-b)

 for exception case see [EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-selop-reserv-allow-b-on-a) |
| EMV_RESERVATION_B_OFFLINE | =5|  reservation variant b (with partial reversal) allowed, no amount increment (Reservierung-Erhoehung) 

 offline allowed (will be without partial reversal)

 according to EMVConf::setTransactionType(): [EMV_TXN_INIT_RESERVATION_B](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-init-reservation-b)

 for exception case see [EMV_CT_SELOP_RESERV_ALLOW_B_ON_A](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-ct-selop-reserv-allow-b-on-a) |

### enum EMVSpecialTip

| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |

| EMV_TIP_YES | =1|  tip (gratuity) allowed: Transactions with [EMV_TXN_TIP](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-txn-tip) are forced online and marked with #EMVSI_GICC_TIPPABLE if applicable  |
| EMV_TIP_MODE_TIPPABLE | =1|  tip (gratuity) same as [EMV_TIP_YES](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-tip-yes) |
| EMV_TIP_NON_REFUSED | =3|  tip (gratuity) allowed if the card holder did not explicitly disliked it, that is there was a tip amount input dialog and she confirmed zero amount.  |

EMV merchant info 


### enum EMVStatusInformation

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| EMV_SI_ONLINE_PIN_REQUIRED | =0x00000001|  this means Online PIN CVM was performed during the transaction (CT: already done in a callback by the app, CTLS: to be performed by the app once the card is out of the field) --> Online PIN processing (host encryption) is required if the transaction is not declined or if there is no fallback.  |
| EMV_SI_SIGNATURE_REQUIRED | =0x00000002|  this means signature CVM was performed and the signature line must be printed on the receipt if the transaction is not declined or if there is no fallback.  |
| EMV_SI_FORCED_ACCEPTANCE | =0x00000004|  Forced acceptance transaction  |
| EMV_SI_USER_DEFINED_CVM | =0x00000008|  user defined CVM, this means that a custom CVM was performed and according to custom/domestic rules additional steps may apply  |
| EMV_SI_ON_DEVICE_CVM | =0x00000010|  An On-Device CVM was performed (Amex: "Mobile CVM", Visa: "Consumer
                                         device CVM"). Caution, obsolete: For VFI-Reader it indicates if CVM has been performed on the consumer device even if transaction flow CVM was no CVM (e.g. because below CVM-Limit). But for VERTEX this bit is set if CD-CVM is indicated in the kernel outcome with exception for Amex. Replaced by [EMV_SI_CONSUMER_DEVICE](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-si-consumer-device) and [EMV_SI_OUTCOME_CD_CVM](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-emv-si-outcome-cd-cvm) with a consistent behaviour.  |
| EMV_SI_CUSTOMER_CARDWITHDRAWL | =0x00000080|   |
| EMV_SI_GICC_TIPPABLE | =0x00000100|  A tip transaction may follow this payment  |
| EMV_SI_PTC_EXCEEDED | =0x00000200|  PIN try counter exceeded  |
| EMV_SI_PIN_FAILURE | =0x00000400|  Last entered offline PIN was wrong  |
| EMV_SI_CONTACTLESS_CHIP | =0x00000800|  A contactless chip transaction  |
| EMV_SI_CONTACTLESS_MSR | =0x00001000|  A contactless magstripe txn  |
| EMV_SI_TORN_CREATED | =0x00002000|  A torn transaction was created (PP3) 

 not used for contact  |
| EMV_SI_TORN_TRY_RECOVER | =0x00004000|  A torn transaction was tried to recover 

 not used for contact  |
| EMV_SI_CONTACTLESS_WAITING | =0x00008000|  The contactless transaction is still in the card waiting phase  |
| EMV_SI_CONTACT_ONGOING | =0x00008000|  The contact transaction is still ongoing  |
| EMV_SI_CTLS_LONG_TAP | =0x00010000|  Contactless "long tap", only appears if transaction goes online, card has to remain in field until [EMV_CTLS_ContinueOnline()](group___f_u_n_c___f_l_o_w.md#function-emv-ctls-continueonline) returned  |
| EMV_SI_ARQC_RESTART_ANY | =0x00020000|  Contactless kernel asks for second activation after online request in any case even in case of online problem (e.g. girocard OUT.ORD=ANY)  |
| EMV_SI_ARQC_RESTART_UTGO | =0x00040000|  Contactless kernel set OUT.ORD to EMV&OTGO and conditions for offline approval are valid. Retap required if unable to go online or script/auth data available.  |
| EMV_SI_CONSUMER_DEVICE | =0x00080000|  Contactless transaction performed by a consumer device (smart phone, tablet, watch) supporting CD-CVM (Consumer Device Cardholder Verification Method).  |
| EMV_SI_CONTACTLESS_ONLY | =0x00100000|  Contactless device, key fob or mini card without alternate interfaces. Note: This bit is derived from various card properties like "switch
                                         interface" or form factor indicators and is not reliable for all schemes. Don't use this information for control flow. It is intended as additional information or for statistics.  |
| EMV_SI_OUTCOME_CD_CVM | =0x00200000|  Contactless set if kernel Outcome Parameter CVM = Confirmation Code Verified (Consumer Device CVM successfully performed, see Book A)  |
| EMV_SI_OUTCOME_RECEIPT | =0x00400000|  Contactless set if kernel Outcome Parameter Receipt = Yes (provide a receipt, see Book A). Note: For instance only supported for MasterCard, girocard, JCB and RuPay.  |
| EMV_SI_WRITE_DS_FAILED | =0x00800000|  Contact Write data storage has failed  |
| EMV_SI_ARQC_RESTART_FORBIDDEN | =0x01000000|  Do not prompt for re-tap, no matter if there are issuer authentication data or scripts. This is a requirement for JCB online outcome neither 2 presentments nor present and hold and other kernels (e.g. Gemalto-PURE). It is also set for kernels that do not process issuer update at all (e.g. MasterCard, Visa, Amex, CUP, ...) and contactless mag. stripe transactions  |
| EMV_SI_ARQC_RESTART_NO_IAUTHD | =0x02000000|  Only prompt for re-tap in case issuer scripts are present, that is discard Issuer Authentication Data (IAuD, tag '91'). This flag is set for Discover and WISE transactions.  |




EMV status information bits returned by [EMVTxn::getEMVStatus()](structvfisdi_1_1_e_m_v_txn.md#function-getemvstatus)

| NFC_POLL_TECH_AB |   0x03|   |
| NFC_POLL_TECH_F_DEP |   0x04|   |
| NFC_POLL_TECH_FELICA |   0x08|   |




NFC polling parameter bitmap 


### enum TECStartOptions

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| TEC_NFC_ENABLE | =0x01|  CTLS, only allowed if [CTS_VAS_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-vas-enable) is NOT set: ADK-NFC is used for detection of contactless cards, options[12..15] determine which NFC technology is enabled.  |
| TEC_VAS_ENABLE | =0x02|  CTLS, only allowed if [CTS_NFC_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-nfc-enable) is NOT set: ADK-NFC is used for Wallet processing.  |
| TEC_EMV_AFTER_NFC_ISO | =0x04|  Relevant only if [CTS_NFC_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-nfc-enable) is set. Perform an EMV transaction if NFC has detected one of the following cards: I_ISO14443A, I_ISO14443B  |
| TEC_VAS_HANDLE_LED_BUZZ | =0x08|  Relevant only if [CTS_VAS_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-vas-enable) is set: Handle LEDs and buzzer if VAS processing failed or VAS only (no subsequent EMV transaction).  |
| TEC_EMV_CTLS_TIMEOUT_AFTER_VAS | =0x10|  Relevant only if [CTS_VAS_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-vas-enable) is set: This option enables the use of a permissible time window to perform a contactless payment after either VAS_DO_PAY or VAS_DO_PAY_DECRYPT_REQ has been detected. The dimension of this time window is configured with the input parameter options[10..11] of the function [cts_StartSelection()](tec_8h.md#function-cts-startselection).  |
| TEC_VAS_DONT_DECRYPT | =0x20|  Relevant only if [CTS_VAS_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-vas-enable) is set: TEC will NOT decrypt the resulting VAS data.  |
| TEC_MSR_AFTER_CTLS_FAIL | =0x40|  Relevant only if options[6..7] is set: Wait for MSR read after CTLS transaction only if that failed.  |
| TEC_NFC_DUTY_CYCLE_OFF | =0x80|  Relevant only if [CTS_NFC_ENABLE](group___t_e_c___s_t_a_r_t___o_p_t_i_o_n_s.md#define-cts-nfc-enable) is set. Ux700 overheat protection (duty cycle) is turned on by default. Can be switched off by this bit.  |
| TEC_PURE_CARD_DETECTION | =0x0100|  Relevant for CTLS only: only detect card, do not perform transaction  |
| TEC_NO_POWERON | =0x0200|  Relevant for CT only (must not be set in conjunction with [TEC_POWERON_AFTER_CTLS_MSR_DEACTIVATION](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-tec-poweron-after-ctls-msr-deactivation)): do not power on inserted card.  |
| TEC_POWERON_AFTER_CTLS_MSR_DEACTIVATION | =0x4000|  Relevant for CT only (must not be set in conjunction with [TEC_NO_POWERON](namespacevfisdi.md#enumvalue-tec-no-poweron)): deactivate CTLS and MRS once chip-card is detected and then power on the chip-card.  |




SDI TEC start options (bit mask) 


### enum TECNFC

| Enumerator | Value | Description |
| ---------- | ----- | ----------- |
| TEC_TECH_A |   0x01|  NFC technology A  |
| TEC_TECH_B |   0x02|  NFC technology B  |
| TEC_TECH_AB |   0x03|  NFC technology A and B  |
| TEC_TECH_F_DEP |   0x04|  NFC technology F_DEP, not supported yet  |
| TEC_TECH_FELICA |   0x08|  NFC technology Felica  |




SDI NFC technologies (bit mask)
